$('#resendForgotPasswordId').hide();
$('#signInId').hide();
	$(document) .ready(function(){
		$('#headerSignBtn, #sitemapSignBtn').click(function(){
			$('#signInId').toggle();
			$(this) .toggleClass('upArrow');
			$('#resendForgotPasswordId').hide();
			$('#resendVerificationId').hide();
			$('#signFormId').data('validator').resetForm();
			$('#resendVerificationMailFormId').data('validator').resetForm();
			$('#forgotPasswordFormId').data('validator').resetForm();
		});
		if($('#loginError').val()){
			$('#signInId').show();
		}
		if($('#facebookMappingMessage').val()){
			$('#signInId').show();
		}
		if($('#followCompanyMessage').val()){
			$('#signInId').show();
		}
		$('#forgotPasswordId').click(function(){
			$('#resendForgotPasswordId').show();
			$('#forgotPasswordFormId').data('validator').resetForm();
			$('#errorMessageId').text('');
			$('#successMessageId').text('');
			$('#signInId').hide();
		});
		$('#verificationId').click(function(){
			$('#resendVerificationId').show();
			$('#resendVerificationMailFormId').data('validator').resetForm();
			$('#signInId').hide();
		});
	});
	
	$(document).live('keyup', function(event){
	    if(event.which === 27) {
	        $('#signInId').hide();
	        $('#resendForgotPasswordId').hide();
	        $('#resendVerificationId').hide();
	    }
	});

$(document).ready(function(){
	$("#signFormId").validate();
	$("signInBtnId").click(function(){
		var validForm = $("#signFormId").valid();
		if(validForm) {
			$("signFormId").submit();
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	});
	
	$('#signFormId').on('keyup', function(e){
		var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : (e.which ? e.which : e.charCode));
		if (keycode == 13){
			e.preventDefault();
			$("#signInBtnId").trigger('click');
		}
	});
	
   	if ($(".thankyouMessage").html().length > 0) {
    	$('.thankyouMessage') .show();
  	}else{
	   $('.thankyouMessage') .hide();
   	}
});

$(function(){
	$(window).scroll(function () {
		if ($(window).scrollTop() > 96) {
            $("#topContainer").css('display', 'block');
            $("#headerWrapperID").css("position","fixed");
        }else{
            $("#topContainer").css('display', 'none');
            $("#headerWrapperID").css("position","static");
        }
	});
	
});

$(document).ready(function(){

	 $('.userMessage') .hide();

	$("#followCompanyDiv").click(function(){
		var onVerified = function(response){
			$.each(response, function(key, value) { 
				$("#operationmessagefollow").text(value);
			});
		};
		AJAX_GET_JSON($(this).data("url"), onVerified);
	});
});

$(document).ready(function(){
	$('#from').attr('readonly','readonly');
	$('#to').attr('readonly','readonly');
	$( "#from" ).datepicker({
		yearRange: "-80:+0",
		changeYear: true,
		changeMonth: true,
		numberOfMonths: 1,
		showOn: "button",
		dateFormat: 'dd/mm/yy',
		buttonImage: "/resources/images/calendar.gif",
		buttonImageOnly: true,
		onClose: function( selectedDate ) {
			$( "#to" ).datepicker( "option", "minDate", selectedDate );
		}
	})
	$( "#from" ).keyup(function(e) {
	    if(e.keyCode == 8 || e.keyCode == 46) {
	        $.datepicker._clearDate(this);
	        $( "#to" ).datepicker( "option",  {
	            minDate: null,
	            maxDate: null} );
	    }
	});
	$( "#to" ).datepicker({
		yearRange: "-80:+0",
		changeYear: true,
		changeMonth: true,
		numberOfMonths: 1,
		showOn: "button",
		dateFormat: 'dd/mm/yy',
		buttonImage: "/resources/images/calendar.gif",
		buttonImageOnly: true,
		onClose: function( selectedDate ) {
			$( "#from" ).datepicker( "option", "maxDate", selectedDate );
		}
	})
	$( "#to" ).keyup(function(e) {
	    if(e.keyCode == 8 || e.keyCode == 46) {
	        $.datepicker._clearDate(this);
	        $( "#from" ).datepicker( "option", {
	            minDate: null,
	            maxDate: null} );
	    }
	});
	
    var setCity = function () { 
		if($('#hiddenLocId').val() != ''){
			var selectedLocation = $('#hiddenLocId').val();
			var select = $('#locationComboId');
				select.find('option[value="'+selectedLocation+'"]').attr("selected", "selected");
		}
		
		var locationValue = $('.locationSel') .find('select option:selected').text();
		$('.locationSel') .find('.selectOutput').text(locationValue);
		
    };
	loadLocationsCallback('locationComboId', setCity);
	
	$("#errorMessage").hide();
	$("#imaAdvanceSearchFormId").validate();
	
	$('#goButtnId').click(function(event){
		$("#errorMessage").hide();
		var expTo = parseInt($("#expToId option:selected").val());
		var expFrom = parseInt($("#expFromId option:selected").val());
		var isBlank=true;
		if($('input:radio:checked').length<1 && $('input:checkbox:checked').length<1 && $('#keyword').val().length<3 && $('#companyName').val().length<3 && 
				$('#locationComboId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#industryId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#from').val() == "" && $('#to').val() == ""
				&& $('#functionId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#expFromId option:selected').val() == ""  && $('#expToId option:selected').val() == "") {
			isBlank=true;
		} else {
			isBlank=false;
		}
		if(isBlank){
			$('#errorMessage').html('Please provide any one of the search criteria.');
		  	$('#errorMessage').show();
		  	return;
		} else if(expFrom != "" && expTo != "" && expFrom > expTo) {
			$('#errorMessage').html('Experience To should be greater than Experience From.');
		  	$('#errorMessage').show();
		  	return;
		} else{
			$('#errorMessage').hide();
			var validationResult = $("#imaAdvanceSearchFormId").valid();
			if(validationResult){
				var keyword = $('#keyword').val();
				var location = '';
				var jobFunction = '';
				var industry = '';
				var jobLocationId = $('#locationComboId option:selected').val();
				var jobFunctionId = $('#functionId option:selected').val();
				var industryId = $('#industryId option:selected').val();
				
				if(keyword == ''){
					$('#keyWordCompare').val("Vacancy");
				}else{
					$('#keyWordCompare').val(keyword);
				}

				if(jobLocationId == ''){
					location = '';
					$('#locationNameCompare').val("India");
					$('#locationName').val(location);
					$('#hiddenLocId').val('');
				}else {
					location = $('#locationComboId option:selected').text();
					location = $.trim(location);
					$('#locationName').val(location);
					$('#hiddenLocId').val(jobLocationId);
					$('#locationNameCompare').val(location);
				}
				
				if(jobFunctionId == ''){
					$('#functionNameCompare').val('');
				}else{
					jobFunction = $('#functionId option:selected').text();
					jobFunction =  $.trim(jobFunction);
					$('#jobFunctionName').val(jobFunction);
					$('#functionNameCompare').val(jobFunction);
				}
				
				if(industryId != ''){
					industry = $('#industryId option:selected').text();
					industry =  $.trim(industry);
					$('#industryName').val(industry);
				}
				var seoUrl = "";
				if(keyword != '' && location !='' && jobFunction !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-"+keyword+"/Careers-"+location+"/Vacancies-"+jobFunction+"/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(keyword != '' && location !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-"+keyword+"/Careers-"+location+"/Jobs-Vacancies-/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(location != '' && jobFunction !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-Vacancy/Careers-"+location+"/Vacancies-"+jobFunction+"/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(keyword != '' && jobFunction !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-"+keyword+"/Careers-India/Vacancies-"+jobFunction+"/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(keyword != ''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-"+keyword+"/Careers-India/Jobs-Vacancies-/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(location !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-Vacancy/Careers-"+location+"/Jobs-Vacancies-/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(jobFunction !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-Vacancy/Careers-India/Vacancies-"+jobFunction+"/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else{
					seoUrl = "/jobs-Vacancy/Careers-India/Jobs-Vacancies-/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}
				submitFormUsingGet('imaAdvanceSearchFormId',seoUrl);
			}
			return false;
		}
		return false;
	});
	$('#imaAdvanceSearchFormId').on('keyup', function(e){
		var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : (e.which ? e.which : e.charCode));
		if (keycode == 13){
			e.preventDefault();
			$("#goButtnId").trigger('click');
		}
	});
});
/**
 * This function creates a bean in backend in first request. in second request it populates the data
 * @param formId
 * @param formUrl
 */
function submitFormUsingGet(formId, formUrl){
	var jQueryFormId = "#" + formId ;
	AJAX_GET_JSON_DATA("/createjobsearchbean", $("#" + formId ).serialize(), function(data){
		$.each(data, function(key, value) { 
			if(key == 'success' && value == 'success'){
				//now send get request
				window.location.href = formUrl;
 			}   
		});
	});
}

function saveSearch() {
	var isBlank=true;
	if($('input:radio:checked').length<1 && $('input:checkbox:checked').length<1 && $('#keyword').val().length<3 && $('#companyName').val().length<3 && 
			$('#locationComboId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#industryId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#from').val() == "" && $('#to').val() == ""
			&& $('#functionId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#expFromId option:selected').val() == ""  && $('#expToId option:selected').val() == "") {
		isBlank=true;
	} else {
		isBlank=false;
	}
	if(isBlank){
  		$('#errorMessage').html('Please provide any one of the search criteria to save search');
	  	$('#errorMessage').show();
	  	return;
 	}
	$('#errorMessage').html('');
	openPopUp('/saveSearch','popUpPageConatiner');
}

', 

var company_index=0;

/* Binding Auto completer */
/* Auto-completer for select job location */
makeAutoCompleter('companyName','/suggestCompany',company_index);

/**
 * source_id--the input field id need to make auto completer
 * add_buton_id-- the add button id
 * destination_id- the place where selected item will be appended along with hidden fields
 * url-- the url path to get json data against input character
 * path_variable-- form field name
 * var -- to hold selected value
 */
function makeAutoCompleter(source_id,purl,index) {
	is_selected = false;
	$('#' + source_id).autocomplete(
			{
				source : function(request, response) {
					$.ajax({
						url :  purl + "?matchString="
								+ request.term,
						dataType : "json",
						success : function(data) {
							response($.map(data, function(v, i) {
								v = v.replace('<b>',"").replace('</b>',"");
								return {
									label : i,
									value : v
								};
							}));
						}
					});
				},
				focus : function(event, ui) {
						$('#'+source_id).val(ui.item.value);
				},
				minLength : 3,
				select : function(event, ui) {
					$('#'+source_id).val(ui.item.value);
					index++;
					return false;
				}
			}).data("ui-autocomplete")._renderItem = function(ul, item) {
		return $("<li>").append("<a>" + item.value + "</a>").appendTo(ul);
	};
}

$(document).ready(function (){
	var rate;
	$(".starRating1").each(function() {
		rate = $(this).data("rating");
		if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
			rate = 1;
		$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
	});
	$("#jobSearchTable_paginate").click(function (){
		$(".starRating1").each(function() {
			rate = $(this).data("rating");
			if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
				rate = 1;
			$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
		});
	});
	$("#narrowbyfilters").click(function (){
		$(".starRating1").each(function() {
			rate = $(this).data("rating");
			if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
				rate = 1;
			$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
		});
	});
	$("#checkAllId").click(function(){
		$('[name="jobIdCheckBox"]').each(function() {
			$(this).prop('checked', true);
		});
	});
	$("#uncheckAllId").click(function(){
		$('[name="jobIdCheckBox"]').each(function() {
			$(this).prop('checked', false);
		});
	});
	$("#sendJobToFriendId").click(function(){
		var jobsList = "";
		var checkedFlag = false;
		$('[name="jobIdCheckBox"]').each(function() {
			if($(this).is(":checked")) {
				jobsList += ($(this).val()+",");
				checkedFlag = true;
			}
		});
		if(checkedFlag) {
			jobsList = jobsList.substring(0,jobsList.length-1);
			openPopUp('/sendJobFriend/'+jobsList,'popUpPageConatiner');
		} else {
			alert("Check atleast one job.");
			return false;
		}
	});
	$("#saveJobsId").click(function(){
		var jobsList = "";
		var checkedFlag = false;
		$('[name="jobIdCheckBox"]').each(function() {
			if($(this).is(":checked")) {
				jobsList += ($(this).val()+",");
				checkedFlag = true;
			}
		});
		if(checkedFlag) {
			jobsList = jobsList.substring(0,jobsList.length-1);
			var onVerified = function(response){
				$.each(response, function(key, value) { 
					if(key="errorMessage")
						$("#saveJobsMessageId").prop("class","errorMessage");
					else
						$("#saveJobsMessageId").prop("class","successMessage");
					AJAX_GET_HTML("/savedJobsByCandidate", "savedJobsDiv");
					$("#saveJobsMessageId").text(value);
					$('#signInId').toggle();
				});
			};
			AJAX_GET_JSON('/saveJobsList/'+jobsList, onVerified);
			return false;
		} else {
			alert("Check atleast one job.");
			return false;
		}
		return false;
	});
	
});
function relevanceClickHandler(){
	$("#relevanceColumn").trigger("click");
	$(".starRating1").each(function() {
		rate = $(this).data("rating");
		if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
			rate = 1;
		$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
	});
}
function dateClickHandler(){
	$("#dateColumn").trigger("click");
	$(".starRating1").each(function() {
		rate = $(this).data("rating");
		if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
			rate = 1;
		$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
	});
}

$(function(){
	$(window).scroll(function () {
		if ($(window).scrollTop() > 96) {
            $("#topContainer").css('display', 'block');
            $("#headerWrapperID").css("position","fixed");
        }else{
            $("#topContainer").css('display', 'none');
            $("#headerWrapperID").css("position","static");
        }
	});
	
});

$(document).ready(function(){
	AJAX_GET_HTML("/savedJobsByCandidate", "savedJobsDiv");
	AJAX_GET_HTML("/savedSearches", "savedSearchesDiv");
	if ($(".userMessage").html().length > 0) {
	  $('.userMessage') .show();
	}else{
	 $('.userMessage') .hide();
	}
	$("#followCompanyDiv").click(function(){
		var onVerified = function(response){
			$.each(response, function(key, value) { 
				$("#operationmessagefollow").text(value);
			});
		};
		AJAX_GET_JSON($(this).data("url"), onVerified);
	});
});

$(document).ready(function(){
	$('#from').attr('readonly','readonly');
	$('#to').attr('readonly','readonly');
	$( "#from" ).datepicker({
		yearRange: "-80:+0",
		changeYear: true,
		changeMonth: true,
		numberOfMonths: 1,
		showOn: "button",
		dateFormat: 'dd/mm/yy',
		buttonImage: "/resources/images/calendar.gif",
		buttonImageOnly: true,
		onClose: function( selectedDate ) {
			$( "#to" ).datepicker( "option", "minDate", selectedDate );
		}
	})
	$( "#from" ).keyup(function(e) {
	    if(e.keyCode == 8 || e.keyCode == 46) {
	        $.datepicker._clearDate(this);
	        $( "#to" ).datepicker( "option",  {
	            minDate: null,
	            maxDate: null} );
	    }
	});
	$( "#to" ).datepicker({
		yearRange: "-80:+0",
		changeYear: true,
		changeMonth: true,
		numberOfMonths: 1,
		showOn: "button",
		dateFormat: 'dd/mm/yy',
		buttonImage: "/resources/images/calendar.gif",
		buttonImageOnly: true,
		onClose: function( selectedDate ) {
			$( "#from" ).datepicker( "option", "maxDate", selectedDate );
		}
	})
	$( "#to" ).keyup(function(e) {
	    if(e.keyCode == 8 || e.keyCode == 46) {
	        $.datepicker._clearDate(this);
	        $( "#from" ).datepicker( "option", {
	            minDate: null,
	            maxDate: null} );
	    }
	});
	
    var setCity = function () { 
		if($('#hiddenLocId').val() != ''){
			var selectedLocation = $('#hiddenLocId').val();
			var select = $('#locationComboId');
				select.find('option[value="'+selectedLocation+'"]').attr("selected", "selected");
		}
		
		var locationValue = $('.locationSel') .find('select option:selected').text();
		$('.locationSel') .find('.selectOutput').text(locationValue);
		
    };
	loadLocationsCallback('locationComboId', setCity);
	
	$("#errorMessage").hide();
	$("#imaAdvanceSearchFormId").validate();
	
	$('#goButtnId').click(function(event){
		$("#errorMessage").hide();
		var expTo = parseInt($("#expToId option:selected").val());
		var expFrom = parseInt($("#expFromId option:selected").val());
		var isBlank=true;
		if($('input:radio:checked').length<1 && $('input:checkbox:checked').length<1 && $('#keyword').val().length<3 && $('#companyName').val().length<3 && 
				$('#locationComboId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#industryId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#from').val() == "" && $('#to').val() == ""
				&& $('#functionId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#expFromId option:selected').val() == ""  && $('#expToId option:selected').val() == "") {
			isBlank=true;
		} else {
			isBlank=false;
		}
		if(isBlank){
			$('#errorMessage').html('Please provide any one of the search criteria.');
		  	$('#errorMessage').show();
		  	return;
		} else if(expFrom != "" && expTo != "" && expFrom > expTo) {
			$('#errorMessage').html('Experience To should be greater than Experience From.');
		  	$('#errorMessage').show();
		  	return;
		} else{
			$('#errorMessage').hide();
			var validationResult = $("#imaAdvanceSearchFormId").valid();
			if(validationResult){
				var keyword = $('#keyword').val();
				var location = '';
				var jobFunction = '';
				var industry = '';
				var jobLocationId = $('#locationComboId option:selected').val();
				var jobFunctionId = $('#functionId option:selected').val();
				var industryId = $('#industryId option:selected').val();
				
				if(keyword == ''){
					$('#keyWordCompare').val("Vacancy");
				}else{
					$('#keyWordCompare').val(keyword);
				}

				if(jobLocationId == ''){
					location = '';
					$('#locationNameCompare').val("India");
					$('#locationName').val(location);
					$('#hiddenLocId').val('');
				}else {
					location = $('#locationComboId option:selected').text();
					location = $.trim(location);
					$('#locationName').val(location);
					$('#hiddenLocId').val(jobLocationId);
					$('#locationNameCompare').val(location);
				}
				
				if(jobFunctionId == ''){
					$('#functionNameCompare').val('');
				}else{
					jobFunction = $('#functionId option:selected').text();
					jobFunction =  $.trim(jobFunction);
					$('#jobFunctionName').val(jobFunction);
					$('#functionNameCompare').val(jobFunction);
				}
				
				if(industryId != ''){
					industry = $('#industryId option:selected').text();
					industry =  $.trim(industry);
					$('#industryName').val(industry);
				}
				var seoUrl = "";
				if(keyword != '' && location !='' && jobFunction !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-"+keyword+"/Careers-"+location+"/Vacancies-"+jobFunction+"/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(keyword != '' && location !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-"+keyword+"/Careers-"+location+"/Jobs-Vacancies-/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(location != '' && jobFunction !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-Vacancy/Careers-"+location+"/Vacancies-"+jobFunction+"/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(keyword != '' && jobFunction !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-"+keyword+"/Careers-India/Vacancies-"+jobFunction+"/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(keyword != ''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-"+keyword+"/Careers-India/Jobs-Vacancies-/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(location !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-Vacancy/Careers-"+location+"/Jobs-Vacancies-/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else if(jobFunction !=''){
					seoUrl = "/jobs-Vacancy/Careers-India/Vacancies-"+jobFunction+"/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}else{
					seoUrl = "/jobs-Vacancy/Careers-India/Jobs-Vacancies-/Naukri/India-jobs-search";
				}
				submitFormUsingGet('imaAdvanceSearchFormId',seoUrl);
			}
			return false;
		}
		return false;
	});
	$('#imaAdvanceSearchFormId').on('keyup', function(e){
		var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : (e.which ? e.which : e.charCode));
		if (keycode == 13){
			e.preventDefault();
			$("#goButtnId").trigger('click');
		}
	});
});
/**
 * This function creates a bean in backend in first request. in second request it populates the data
 * @param formId
 * @param formUrl
 */
function submitFormUsingGet(formId, formUrl){
	var jQueryFormId = "#" + formId ;
	AJAX_GET_JSON_DATA("/createjobsearchbean", $("#" + formId ).serialize(), function(data){
		$.each(data, function(key, value) { 
			if(key == 'success' && value == 'success'){
				//now send get request
				window.location.href = formUrl;
 			}   
		});
	});
}

function saveSearch() {
	var isBlank=true;
	if($('input:radio:checked').length<1 && $('input:checkbox:checked').length<1 && $('#keyword').val().length<3 && $('#companyName').val().length<3 && 
			$('#locationComboId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#industryId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#from').val() == "" && $('#to').val() == ""
			&& $('#functionId option:selected').val() == "" && $('#expFromId option:selected').val() == ""  && $('#expToId option:selected').val() == "") {
		isBlank=true;
	} else {
		isBlank=false;
	}
	if(isBlank){
  		$('#errorMessage').html('Please provide any one of the search criteria to save search');
	  	$('#errorMessage').show();
	  	return;
 	}
	$('#errorMessage').html('');
	openPopUp('/saveSearch','popUpPageConatiner');
}

', 

var company_index=0;

/* Binding Auto completer */
/* Auto-completer for select job location */
makeAutoCompleter('companyName','/suggestCompany',company_index);

/**
 * source_id--the input field id need to make auto completer
 * add_buton_id-- the add button id
 * destination_id- the place where selected item will be appended along with hidden fields
 * url-- the url path to get json data against input character
 * path_variable-- form field name
 * var -- to hold selected value
 */
function makeAutoCompleter(source_id,purl,index) {
	is_selected = false;
	$('#' + source_id).autocomplete(
			{
				source : function(request, response) {
					$.ajax({
						url :  purl + "?matchString="
								+ request.term,
						dataType : "json",
						success : function(data) {
							response($.map(data, function(v, i) {
								v = v.replace('<b>',"").replace('</b>',"");
								return {
									label : i,
									value : v
								};
							}));
						}
					});
				},
				focus : function(event, ui) {
						$('#'+source_id).val(ui.item.value);
				},
				minLength : 3,
				select : function(event, ui) {
					$('#'+source_id).val(ui.item.value);
					index++;
					return false;
				}
			}).data("ui-autocomplete")._renderItem = function(ul, item) {
		return $("<li>").append("<a>" + item.value + "</a>").appendTo(ul);
	};
}

', 
$(document).ready(function (){
	var rate;
	$(".starRating1").each(function() {
		rate = $(this).data("rating");
		if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
			rate = 1;
		$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
	});
	$("#jobSearchTable_paginate").click(function (){
		$(".starRating1").each(function() {
			rate = $(this).data("rating");
			if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
				rate = 1;
			$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
		});
	});
	$("#narrowbyfilters").click(function (){
		$(".starRating1").each(function() {
			rate = $(this).data("rating");
			if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
				rate = 1;
			$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
		});
	});
	$("#checkAllId").click(function(){
		$('[name="jobIdCheckBox"]').each(function() {
			$(this).prop('checked', true);
		});
	});
	$("#uncheckAllId").click(function(){
		$('[name="jobIdCheckBox"]').each(function() {
			$(this).prop('checked', false);
		});
	});
	$("#sendJobToFriendId").click(function(){
		var jobsList = "";
		var checkedFlag = false;
		$('[name="jobIdCheckBox"]').each(function() {
			if($(this).is(":checked")) {
				jobsList += ($(this).val()+",");
				checkedFlag = true;
			}
		});
		if(checkedFlag) {
			jobsList = jobsList.substring(0,jobsList.length-1);
			openPopUp('/sendJobFriend/'+jobsList,'popUpPageConatiner');
		} else {
			alert("Check atleast one job.");
			return false;
		}
	});
	$("#saveJobsId").click(function(){
		var jobsList = "";
		var checkedFlag = false;
		$('[name="jobIdCheckBox"]').each(function() {
			if($(this).is(":checked")) {
				jobsList += ($(this).val()+",");
				checkedFlag = true;
			}
		});
		if(checkedFlag) {
			jobsList = jobsList.substring(0,jobsList.length-1);
			var onVerified = function(response){
				$.each(response, function(key, value) { 
					if(key="errorMessage")
						$("#saveJobsMessageId").prop("class","errorMessage");
					else
						$("#saveJobsMessageId").prop("class","successMessage");
					AJAX_GET_HTML("/savedJobsByCandidate", "savedJobsDiv");
					$("#saveJobsMessageId").text(value);
					$('#signInId').toggle();
				});
			};
			AJAX_GET_JSON('/saveJobsList/'+jobsList, onVerified);
			return false;
		} else {
			alert("Check atleast one job.");
			return false;
		}
		return false;
	});
	
});
function relevanceClickHandler(){
	$("#relevanceColumn").trigger("click");
	$(".starRating1").each(function() {
		rate = $(this).data("rating");
		if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
			rate = 1;
		$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
	});
}
function dateClickHandler(){
	$("#dateColumn").trigger("click");
	$(".starRating1").each(function() {
		rate = $(this).data("rating");
		if(rate=="undefined" || rate == null || rate<1)
			rate = 1;
		$('span#'+this.id) .html('<img src="/resources/images/rating'+rate+'.png" /><span style="display:none">'+rate+ '</span>');
	});
}

', 
$(document).ready(function() {
	loadLocationsName('locationDropdownId');
	var fileError = '';
	$("#fileErrorMsgId").html(fileError);
	$('#fileErrorMsgId').show();
	$("#populateCVFormId").validate();
	$('#uploadId').click(function(e){
		$("#fileErrorMsgId").html('');
		$('#fileErrorMsgId').hide();
		var validationResult = $("#populateCVFormId").valid();
		if(validationResult){
			$("#populateCVFormId").submit();
		}
	});
	
	$('#populateCVFormId').on('keyup', function(e){
		var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : (e.which ? e.which : e.charCode));
		if (keycode == 13){
			e.preventDefault();
			$("#uploadId").trigger('click');
		}
	});	
});
', 
', 
	.fileSizeError {
		padding-left:20px !important; background-position:2px 2px !important;
	}
